  [Agent Output] === app.py ===
from flask import Flask, redirect, url_for, request, render_template, abort
import os
from datetime import datetime

app = Flask(__name__)
app.secret_key = 'dev-secret-key'

DATA_DIR = "data"

# File paths
GALLERIES_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "galleries.txt")
EXHIBITIONS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "exhibitions.txt")
ARTIFACTS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "artifacts.txt")
GUIDES_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "audio_guides.txt")
TICKETS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "tickets.txt")
EVENTS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "events.txt")
REGISTRATIONS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "event_registrations.txt")

# --- HELPERS ---
def read_pipe_delimited(filepath):
    if not os.path.exists(filepath):
        return []
    with open(filepath, encoding="utf-8") as f:
        lines = [line.strip() for line in f if line.strip()]
    rows = [line.split("|") for line in lines]
    return rows

def write_pipe_delimited(filepath, rows):
    with open(filepath, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for row in rows:
            f.write("|".join(row)+"\n")

# --- ROUTES ---

@app.route("/", methods=["GET"])
def root_redirect():
    return redirect(url_for("dashboard"))

@app.route("/dashboard", methods=["GET"])
def dashboard():
    # summary counts for context
    exhibitions = read_pipe_delimited(EXHIBITIONS_F)
    total_exhibitions = len(exhibitions)
    # active exhibitions: end_date >= today
    now = datetime.now().date()
    active_exhibitions = 0
    for ex in exhibitions:
        if len(ex) >= 6:
            try:
                end_date = datetime.strptime(ex[5], "%Y-%m-%d").date()
                if end_date >= now:
                    active_exhibitions += 1
            except Exception:
                pass

    return render_template("dashboard.html",
        total_exhibitions=total_exhibitions,
        active_exhibitions=active_exhibitions
    )

@app.route("/artifact_catalog", methods=["GET", "POST"])
def artifact_catalog():
    search_query = ""
    filters = {}
    if request.method == "POST":
        search_query = request.form.get("search_query", "").strip()
    else:
        search_query = request.args.get("search_query", "").strip()
    # For filters, assume keys come as filter_key=value
    for key in request.args:
        if key != "search_query":
            filters[key] = request.args.get(key)
    artifacts = []
    rows = read_pipe_delimited(ARTIFACTS_F)
    # fields: artifact_name|gallery_id|storage_location|date_acquired|created_by
    for r in rows:
        if len(r) < 5:
            continue
        if search_query:
            if search_query.lower() not in r[0].lower() and search_query.lower() not in r[1].lower():
                continue
        # TODO: apply other filters if any
        artifacts.append({
            "artifact_name": r[0],
            "gallery_id": r[1],
            "storage_location": r[2],
            "date_acquired": r[3],
            "created_by": r[4],
        })
    return render_template("artifact_catalog.html", artifacts=artifacts, search_query=search_query, filters=filters)

@app.route("/exhibition/<int:exhibition_id>", methods=["GET"])
def exhibition_details(exhibition_id):
    exhibitions = read_pipe_delimited(EXHIBITIONS_F)
    exhibition = None
    for ex in exhibitions:
        try:
            if int(ex[0]) == exhibition_id:
                exhibition = ex
                break
        except Exception:
            continue
    if exhibition is None:
        abort(404, "Exhibition not found")

    # fields: exhibition_id|title|description|gallery_id|exhibition_type|start_date|end_date|curator_name
    artifacts_rows = read_pipe_delimited(ARTIFACTS_F)
    artifacts = []
    gallery_id = exhibition[3] if len(exhibition) > 3 else ""
    for art in artifacts_rows:
        if len(art) > 1 and art[1] == gallery_id:
            artifacts.append({
                "artifact_name": art[0],
                "storage_location": art[2],
                "date_acquired": art[3],
                "created_by": art[4],
            })

    exhibition_dict = {
        "exhibition_id": exhibition[0],
        "title": exhibition[1],
        "description": exhibition[2],
        "gallery_id": exhibition[3],
        "exhibition_type": exhibition[4],
        "start_date": exhibition[5],
        "end_date": exhibition[6],
        "curator_name": exhibition[7] if len(exhibition) > 7 else ""
    }
    return render_template("exhibition_details.html", exhibition=exhibition_dict, artifacts=artifacts)

@app.route("/tickets", methods=["GET"])
def visitor_tickets():
    # tickets.txt fields:
    # visit_date|visit_time|number_of_tickets|visitor_name|visitor_email|purchase_date
    tickets_rows = read_pipe_delimited(TICKETS_F)
    ticket_types = set()
    tickets = []
    for t in tickets_rows:
        if len(t) < 6:
            continue
        tickets.append({
            "visit_date": t[0],
            "visit_time": t[1],
            "number_of_tickets": t[2],
            "visitor_name": t[3],
            "visitor_email": t[4],
            "purchase_date": t[5]
        })
        ticket_types.add(t[2])

    ticket_types = list(ticket_types)
    return render_template("visitor_tickets.html", tickets=tickets, ticket_types=ticket_types)

@app.route("/events", methods=["GET", "POST"])
def virtual_events():
    current_user = "visitor_mary"  # TODO: authentication placeholder
    events_rows = read_pipe_delimited(EVENTS_F)
    registrations_rows = read_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F)

    if request.method == "POST":
        # Either register or cancel
        action = request.form.get("action")
        if action == "cancel":
            registration_id = request.form.get("registration_id")
            if registration_id:
                registrations_rows = [r for r in registrations_rows if r[0] != registration_id or r[2] != current_user]
                write_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F, registrations_rows)
            return redirect(url_for("virtual_events"))
        else:
            abort(400)

    # On GET, list virtual events
    virtual_events_list = []
    for e in events_rows:
        if len(e) < 7:
            continue
        event_type = e[4].lower()
        if event_type == "virtual":
            virtual_events_list.append({
                "event_id": e[0],
                "title": e[1],
                "date": e[2],
                "time": e[3],
                "event_type": e[4],
                "speaker": e[5],
                "seats": e[6] if len(e) > 6 else "",
                "description": e[7] if len(e) > 7 else ""
            })

    # Map registrations for current user: event_id -> registration_id
    regs_map = {r[1]: r[0] for r in registrations_rows if len(r) > 2 and r[2] == current_user}

    return render_template("virtual_events.html", events=virtual_events_list, registrations=regs_map, current_user=current_user)

@app.route("/events/register/<int:event_id>", methods=["GET"])
def register_event(event_id):
    current_user = "visitor_mary"
    registrations_rows = read_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F)
    # Check if already registered
    for r in registrations_rows:
        if len(r) > 2 and r[1] == str(event_id) and r[2] == current_user:
            return redirect(url_for("virtual_events"))
    reg_ids = [int(r[0]) for r in registrations_rows if r[0].isdigit()]
    new_id = str(max(reg_ids)+1 if reg_ids else 1)
    registration_date = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
    registrations_rows.append([new_id, str(event_id), current_user, registration_date])
    write_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F, registrations_rows)
    return redirect(url_for("virtual_events"))

@app.route("/events/cancel/<int:registration_id>", methods=["POST"])
def cancel_registration(registration_id):
    current_user = "visitor_mary"
    registrations_rows = read_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F)
    new_regs = [r for r in registrations_rows if not (r[0] == str(registration_id) and r[2] == current_user)]
    write_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F, new_regs)
    return redirect(url_for("virtual_events"))

@app.route("/audio_guides", methods=["GET"])
def audio_guides():
    filter_language = request.args.get("filter_language", "").lower()
    guides_rows = read_pipe_delimited(GUIDES_F)
    guides = []
    for g in guides_rows:
        # guide_id | exhibit_number | language | script | narrator | created_by
        if len(g) < 6:
            continue
        lang = g[2].lower()
        if filter_language and lang != filter_language:
            continue
        guides.append({
            "guide_id": g[0],
            "exhibit_number": g[1],
            "language": g[2],
            "script": g[3],
            "narrator": g[4],
            "created_by": g[5]
        })
    return render_template("audio_guides.html", audio_guides=guides, filter_language=filter_language)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app.run(port=5000, debug=True)

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. `users.txt`
- Filename: `data/users.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `username`
- Purpose: Stores usernames authorized in the system.
- Examples:
  ```
  curator_john
  visitor_mary
  curator_sarah
  ```

---

### 2. `galleries.txt`
- Filename: `data/galleries.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `gallery_id`
  - `gallery_name`
  - `floor`
  - `capacity`
  - `theme`
  - `status`
- Purpose: Information about museum galleries.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|Ancient Civilizations Hall|1|50|Ancient|Open
  2|Modern Art Wing|2|30|Modern|Open
  3|Science Discovery Center|3|40|Science|Renovation
  ```

---

### 3. `exhibitions.txt`
- Filename: `data/exhibitions.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `exhibition_id`
  - `title`
  - `description`
  - `gallery_id`
  - `exhibition_type`
  - `start_date`
  - `end_date`
  - `curator_name`
  - `created_by`
- Purpose: Museum exhibitions data.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|Egyptian Treasures|Ancient artifacts from Egypt|1|Permanent|2024-01-01|2025-12-31|Dr. Smith|curator_john
  2|Pop Art Revolution|Contemporary pop art collection|2|Temporary|2024-11-01|2024-12-31|Lisa Chen|curator_sarah
  3|Virtual Space Exploration|Online space exhibition|2|Virtual|2024-10-01|2025-03-31|Mark Johnson|curator_john
  ```

---

### 4. `artifacts.txt`
- Filename: `data/artifacts.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `artifact_id`
  - `artifact_name`
  - `period`
  - `origin`
  - `description`
  - `exhibition_id`
  - `storage_location`
  - `acquisition_date`
  - `added_by`
- Purpose: Detailed artifact information.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|Golden Mask of Tutankhamun|Ancient|Egypt|Famous golden funeral mask|1|A-101|2020-05-15|curator_john
  2|Warhol Soup Cans|Contemporary|USA|Iconic pop art piece|2|B-205|2023-08-20|curator_sarah
  3|Roman Amphora|Ancient|Italy|Ancient storage vessel|1|A-103|2019-11-10|curator_john
  ```

---

### 5. `audioguides.txt`
- Filename: `data/audioguides.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `guide_id`
  - `exhibit_number`
  - `title`
  - `language`
  - `duration`
  - `script`
  - `narrator`
  - `created_by`
- Purpose: Audio guide content for exhibits.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|101|Introduction to Egyptian Art|English|5|Welcome to the Egyptian exhibition...|James Brown|curator_john
  2|101|Introducci  n al Arte Egipcio|Spanish|5|Bienvenido a la exhibici  n egipcia...|Maria Garcia|curator_john
  3|205|Pop Art Explained|English|7|Pop art emerged in the 1950s...|Sarah Williams|curator_sarah
  ```

---

### 6. `tickets.txt`
- Filename: `data/tickets.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `ticket_id`
  - `username`
  - `ticket_type`
  - `visit_date`
  - `visit_time`
  - `number_of_tickets`
  - `price`
  - `visitor_name`
  - `visitor_email`
  - `purchase_date`
- Purpose: Visitor ticket sales data.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|visitor_mary|Standard|2024-11-25|11:00 AM|2|30|Mary Johnson|mary@email.com|2024-11-20
  2|visitor_mary|VIP|2024-12-01|1:00 PM|1|50|Mary Johnson|mary@email.com|2024-11-20
  3|visitor_tom|Student|2024-11-22|9:00 AM|1|10|Tom Lee|tom@email.com|2024-11-18
  ```

---

### 7. `events.txt`
- Filename: `data/events.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `event_id`
  - `title`
  - `date`
  - `time`
  - `event_type`
  - `speaker`
  - `capacity`
  - `description`
  - `created_by`
- Purpose: Virtual museum events.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|Ancient Egypt Webinar|2024-12-05|2:00 PM|Webinar|Dr. Smith|100|Deep dive into Egyptian culture|curator_john
  2|Meet the Artist: Pop Art|2024-11-30|6:00 PM|Artist Talk|Andy Williams|50|Discussion with contemporary artist|curator_sarah
  3|Virtual Museum Tour|2024-12-10|10:00 AM|Virtual Tour|Lisa Chen|200|Guided tour of entire museum|curator_john
  ```

---

### 8. `event_registrations.txt`
- Filename: `data/event_registrations.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `registration_id`
  - `event_id`
  - `username`
  - `registration_date`
- Purpose: Records registrations for virtual events.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|1|visitor_mary|2024-11-20
  2|2|visitor_mary|2024-11-21
  3|1|visitor_tom|2024-11-19
  ```

---

### 9. `collection_logs.txt`
- Filename: `data/collection_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `log_id`
  - `artifact_id`
  - `activity_type`
  - `date`
  - `notes`
  - `condition`
  - `curator`
- Purpose: Logs artifact-related activities and condition.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|1|Inspection|2024-11-15|Routine quarterly inspection|Excellent|curator_john
  2|1|Cleaning|2024-11-16|Professional cleaning performed|Excellent|curator_john
  3|2|Photography|2024-10-20|High-resolution images taken|Good|curator_sarah
  4|3|Restoration|2024-09-10|Minor crack repair completed|Good|curator_john
  ```

=== app.py ===
from flask import Flask, redirect, url_for, request, render_template, abort
import os
from datetime import datetime

app = Flask(__name__)
app.secret_key = 'dev-secret-key'

DATA_DIR = "data"

# File paths
GALLERIES_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "galleries.txt")
EXHIBITIONS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "exhibitions.txt")
ARTIFACTS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "artifacts.txt")
GUIDES_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "audio_guides.txt")
TICKETS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "tickets.txt")
EVENTS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "events.txt")
REGISTRATIONS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "event_registrations.txt")

# --- HELPERS ---
def read_pipe_delimited(filepath):
    if not os.path.exists(filepath):
        return []
    with open(filepath, encoding="utf-8") as f:
        lines = [line.strip() for line in f if line.strip()]
    rows = [line.split("|") for line in lines]
    return rows

def write_pipe_delimited(filepath, rows):
    with open(filepath, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for row in rows:
            f.write("|".join(row)+"\n")

# --- ROUTES ---

@app.route("/", methods=["GET"])
def root_redirect():
    return redirect(url_for("dashboard"))

@app.route("/dashboard", methods=["GET"])
def dashboard():
    # summary counts for context
    exhibitions = read_pipe_delimited(EXHIBITIONS_F)
    total_exhibitions = len(exhibitions)
    # active exhibitions: end_date >= today
    now = datetime.now().date()
    active_exhibitions = 0
    for ex in exhibitions:
        if len(ex) >= 6:
            try:
                end_date = datetime.strptime(ex[5], "%Y-%m-%d").date()
                if end_date >= now:
                    active_exhibitions += 1
            except Exception:
                pass

    return render_template("dashboard.html",
        total_exhibitions=total_exhibitions,
        active_exhibitions=active_exhibitions
    )

@app.route("/artifact_catalog", methods=["GET", "POST"])
def artifact_catalog():
    search_query = ""
    filters = {}
    if request.method == "POST":
        search_query = request.form.get("search_query", "").strip()
    else:
        search_query = request.args.get("search_query", "").strip()
    # For filters, assume keys come as filter_key=value
    for key in request.args:
        if key != "search_query":
            filters[key] = request.args.get(key)
    artifacts = []
    rows = read_pipe_delimited(ARTIFACTS_F)
    # fields: artifact_name|gallery_id|storage_location|date_acquired|created_by
    for r in rows:
        if len(r) < 5:
            continue
        if search_query:
            if search_query.lower() not in r[0].lower() and search_query.lower() not in r[1].lower():
                continue
        # TODO: apply other filters if any
        artifacts.append({
            "artifact_name": r[0],
            "gallery_id": r[1],
            "storage_location": r[2],
            "date_acquired": r[3],
            "created_by": r[4],
        })
    return render_template("artifact_catalog.html", artifacts=artifacts, search_query=search_query, filters=filters)

@app.route("/exhibition/<int:exhibition_id>", methods=["GET"])
def exhibition_details(exhibition_id):
    exhibitions = read_pipe_delimited(EXHIBITIONS_F)
    exhibition = None
    for ex in exhibitions:
        try:
            if int(ex[0]) == exhibition_id:
                exhibition = ex
                break
        except Exception:
            continue
    if exhibition is None:
        abort(404, "Exhibition not found")

    # fields: exhibition_id|title|description|gallery_id|exhibition_type|start_date|end_date|curator_name
    artifacts_rows = read_pipe_delimited(ARTIFACTS_F)
    artifacts = []
    gallery_id = exhibition[3] if len(exhibition) > 3 else ""
    for art in artifacts_rows:
        if len(art) > 1 and art[1] == gallery_id:
            artifacts.append({
                "artifact_name": art[0],
                "storage_location": art[2],
                "date_acquired": art[3],
                "created_by": art[4],
            })

    exhibition_dict = {
        "exhibition_id": exhibition[0],
        "title": exhibition[1],
        "description": exhibition[2],
        "gallery_id": exhibition[3],
        "exhibition_type": exhibition[4],
        "start_date": exhibition[5],
        "end_date": exhibition[6],
        "curator_name": exhibition[7] if len(exhibition) > 7 else ""
    }
    return render_template("exhibition_details.html", exhibition=exhibition_dict, artifacts=artifacts)

@app.route("/tickets", methods=["GET"])
def visitor_tickets():
    # tickets.txt fields:
    # visit_date|visit_time|number_of_tickets|visitor_name|visitor_email|purchase_date
    tickets_rows = read_pipe_delimited(TICKETS_F)
    ticket_types = set()
    tickets = []
    for t in tickets_rows:
        if len(t) < 6:
            continue
        tickets.append({
            "visit_date": t[0],
            "visit_time": t[1],
            "number_of_tickets": t[2],
            "visitor_name": t[3],
            "visitor_email": t[4],
            "purchase_date": t[5]
        })
        ticket_types.add(t[2])

    ticket_types = list(ticket_types)
    return render_template("visitor_tickets.html", tickets=tickets, ticket_types=ticket_types)

@app.route("/events", methods=["GET", "POST"])
def virtual_events():
    current_user = "visitor_mary"  # TODO: authentication placeholder
    events_rows = read_pipe_delimited(EVENTS_F)
    registrations_rows = read_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F)

    if request.method == "POST":
        # Either register or cancel
        action = request.form.get("action")
        if action == "cancel":
            registration_id = request.form.get("registration_id")
            if registration_id:
                registrations_rows = [r for r in registrations_rows if r[0] != registration_id or r[2] != current_user]
                write_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F, registrations_rows)
            return redirect(url_for("virtual_events"))
        else:
            abort(400)

    # On GET, list virtual events
    virtual_events_list = []
    for e in events_rows:
        if len(e) < 7:
            continue
        event_type = e[4].lower()
        if event_type == "virtual":
            virtual_events_list.append({
                "event_id": e[0],
                "title": e[1],
                "date": e[2],
                "time": e[3],
                "event_type": e[4],
                "speaker": e[5],
                "seats": e[6] if len(e) > 6 else "",
                "description": e[7] if len(e) > 7 else ""
            })

    # Map registrations for current user: event_id -> registration_id
    regs_map = {r[1]: r[0] for r in registrations_rows if len(r) > 2 and r[2] == current_user}

    return render_template("virtual_events.html", events=virtual_events_list, registrations=regs_map, current_user=current_user)

@app.route("/events/register/<int:event_id>", methods=["GET"])
def register_event(event_id):
    current_user = "visitor_mary"
    registrations_rows = read_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F)
    # Check if already registered
    for r in registrations_rows:
        if len(r) > 2 and r[1] == str(event_id) and r[2] == current_user:
            return redirect(url_for("virtual_events"))
    reg_ids = [int(r[0]) for r in registrations_rows if r[0].isdigit()]
    new_id = str(max(reg_ids)+1 if reg_ids else 1)
    registration_date = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
    registrations_rows.append([new_id, str(event_id), current_user, registration_date])
    write_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F, registrations_rows)
    return redirect(url_for("virtual_events"))

@app.route("/events/cancel/<int:registration_id>", methods=["POST"])
def cancel_registration(registration_id):
    current_user = "visitor_mary"
    registrations_rows = read_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F)
    new_regs = [r for r in registrations_rows if not (r[0] == str(registration_id) and r[2] == current_user)]
    write_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F, new_regs)
    return redirect(url_for("virtual_events"))

@app.route("/audio_guides", methods=["GET"])
def audio_guides():
    filter_language = request.args.get("filter_language", "").lower()
    guides_rows = read_pipe_delimited(GUIDES_F)
    guides = []
    for g in guides_rows:
        # guide_id | exhibit_number | language | script | narrator | created_by
        if len(g) < 6:
            continue
        lang = g[2].lower()
        if filter_language and lang != filter_language:
            continue
        guides.append({
            "guide_id": g[0],
            "exhibit_number": g[1],
            "language": g[2],
            "script": g[3],
            "narrator": g[4],
            "created_by": g[5]
        })
    return render_template("audio_guides.html", audio_guides=guides, filter_language=filter_language)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app.run(port=5000, debug=True)

# Design Specification for VirtualMuseum Web Application

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

| Route Path                         | Function Name              | HTTP Method(s) | Template Rendered         | Context Variables (Name: Type)                                  |
|----------------------------------|----------------------------|----------------|---------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------|
| `/`                              | `root_redirect`             | GET            | Redirect to `/dashboard`  | None                                                           |
| `/dashboard`                     | `dashboard`                 | GET            | `dashboard.html`          | `total_exhibitions`: int, `active_exhibitions`: int           |
| `/artifacts`                     | `artifact_catalog`          | GET, POST      | `artifact_catalog.html`   | `artifacts`: list of dict, `search_query`: str, `filters`: dict|
| `/exhibitions`                   | `exhibitions`               | GET, POST      | `exhibitions.html`        | `exhibitions`: list of dict, `filter_type`: str                |
| `/exhibition/<int:exhibition_id>` | `exhibition_details`          | GET            | `exhibition_details.html` | `exhibition`: dict, `artifacts`: list of dict                  |
| `/tickets`                      | `visitor_tickets`           | GET, POST      | `visitor_tickets.html`    | `tickets`: list of dict, `ticket_types`: list of str           |
| `/events`                       | `virtual_events`            | GET, POST      | `virtual_events.html`     | `events`: list of dict, `registrations`: list of dict, `user`: str|
| `/events/register/<int:event_id>` | `register_event`             | POST           | Redirect to `/events`     | None                                                           |
| `/events/cancel/<int:registration_id>` | `cancel_registration`        | POST           | Redirect to `/events`     | None                                                           |
| `/audio-guides`                 | `audio_guides`              | GET, POST      | `audio_guides.html`       | `audio_guides`: list of dict, `filter_language`: str            |

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. `users.txt`
- Filename: `data/users.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `username`
- Purpose: Stores usernames authorized in the system.
- Examples:
  ```
  curator_john
  visitor_mary
  curator_sarah
  ```

---

### 2. `galleries.txt`
- Filename: `data/galleries.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `gallery_id`
  - `gallery_name`
  - `floor`
  - `capacity`
  - `theme`
  - `status`
- Purpose: Information about museum galleries.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|Ancient Civilizations Hall|1|50|Ancient|Open
  2|Modern Art Wing|2|30|Modern|Open
  3|Science Discovery Center|3|40|Science|Renovation
  ```

---

### 3. `exhibitions.txt`
- Filename: `data/exhibitions.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `exhibition_id`
  - `title`
  - `description`
  - `gallery_id`
  - `exhibition_type`
  - `start_date`
  - `end_date`
  - `curator_name`
  - `created_by`
- Purpose: Museum exhibitions data.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|Egyptian Treasures|Ancient artifacts from Egypt|1|Permanent|2024-01-01|2025-12-31|Dr. Smith|curator_john
  2|Pop Art Revolution|Contemporary pop art collection|2|Temporary|2024-11-01|2024-12-31|Lisa Chen|curator_sarah
  3|Virtual Space Exploration|Online space exhibition|2|Virtual|2024-10-01|2025-03-31|Mark Johnson|curator_john
  ```

---

### 4. `artifacts.txt`
- Filename: `data/artifacts.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `artifact_id`
  - `artifact_name`
  - `period`
  - `origin`
  - `description`
  - `exhibition_id`
  - `storage_location`
  - `acquisition_date`
  - `added_by`
- Purpose: Detailed artifact information.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|Golden Mask of Tutankhamun|Ancient|Egypt|Famous golden funeral mask|1|A-101|2020-05-15|curator_john
  2|Warhol Soup Cans|Contemporary|USA|Iconic pop art piece|2|B-205|2023-08-20|curator_sarah
  3|Roman Amphora|Ancient|Italy|Ancient storage vessel|1|A-103|2019-11-10|curator_john
  ```

---

- Filename: `data/audioguides.txt`

  - `exhibit_number`
  - `title`
  - `language`
  - `duration`
  - `script`
  - `narrator`
  - `created_by`
- Purpose: Audio guide content for exhibits.

  1|101|Introduction to Egyptian Art|English|5|Welcome to the Egyptian exhibition...|James Brown|curator_john
  2|101|Introducci  n al Arte Egipcio|Spanish|5|Bienvenido a la exhibici  n egipcia...|Maria Garcia|curator_john
  3|205|Pop Art Explained|English|7|Pop art emerged in the 1950s...|Sarah Williams|curator_sarah
  ```

### 6. `tickets.txt`
- Filename: `data/tickets.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):

  2|visitor_mary|VIP|2024-12-01|1:00 PM|1|50|Mary Johnson|mary@email.com|2024-11-20

  [Agent Output] === app.py ===
from flask import Flask, redirect, url_for, request, render_template, abort
import os
from datetime import datetime

app = Flask(__name__)
app.secret_key = 'dev-secret-key'

DATA_DIR = "data"

# Paths
ARTIFACTS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "artifacts.txt")
EXHIBITIONS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "exhibitions.txt")
TICKETS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "tickets.txt")
EVENTS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "events.txt")
REGISTRATIONS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "event_registrations.txt")
AUDIO_GUIDES_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "audioguides.txt")

# Helpers

def read_pipe_delimited(filepath):
    if not os.path.exists(filepath):
        return []
    with open(filepath, encoding="utf-8") as f:
        return [line.strip().split('|') for line in f if line.strip()]

def write_pipe_delimited(filepath, rows):
    with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        for row in rows:
            f.write('|'.join(row)+'\n')

# Routes

@app.route('/')
def root_redirect():
    return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))

@app.route('/dashboard')
def dashboard():
    exhibitions = read_pipe_delimited(EXHIBITIONS_F)
    total_exhibitions = len(exhibitions)
    now = datetime.now().date()
    active_exhibitions = 0
    for ex in exhibitions:
        if len(ex) > 6:
            try:
                end_date = datetime.strptime(ex[6], '%Y-%m-%d').date()
                if end_date >= now:
                    active_exhibitions += 1
            except:
                pass
    return render_template('dashboard.html', total_exhibitions=total_exhibitions, active_exhibitions=active_exhibitions)

@app.route('/artifact_catalog', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def artifact_catalog():
    search_query = ''
    filters = {}
    if request.method == 'POST':
        search_query = request.form.get('search_query', '').strip()
    else:
        search_query = request.args.get('search_query', '').strip()
    # Filters from args
    for k,v in request.args.items():
        if k != 'search_query':
            filters[k] = v
    artifacts = []
    rows = read_pipe_delimited(ARTIFACTS_F)
    # artifact_name | origin | description | exhibition_id | storage_location
    for r in rows:
        if len(r) < 5:
            continue
        if search_query and search_query.lower() not in r[0].lower() and search_query.lower() not in r[3].lower():
            continue
        artifacts.append({
            'artifact_name': r[0],
            'origin': r[1],
            'description': r[2],
            'exhibition_id': r[3],
            'storage_location': r[4],
        })
    return render_template('artifact_catalog.html', artifacts=artifacts, search_query=search_query, filters=filters)

@app.route('/exhibitions', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def exhibitions():
    exhibitions_rows = read_pipe_delimited(EXHIBITIONS_F)
    exhibitions = []
    if request.method == 'GET':
        type_filter = request.args.get('filter_type','').lower()
        for row in exhibitions_rows:
            if len(row) < 8:
                continue
            if type_filter and row[4].lower() != type_filter:
                continue
            exhibitions.append({
                'exhibition_id': int(row[0]),
                'title': row[1],
                'description': row[2],
                'gallery_id': row[3],
                'exhibition_type': row[4],
                'start_date': row[5],
                'end_date': row[6],
                'curator_name': row[7],
            })
        return render_template('exhibitions.html', exhibitions=exhibitions, filter_type=type_filter)
    else:
        exhibition_id = request.form.get('exhibition_id')
        if not exhibition_id or not exhibition_id.isdigit():
            abort(400)
        exhibition_id = int(exhibition_id)
        exhibition = None
        for row in exhibitions_rows:
            if len(row)>0 and row[0].isdigit() and int(row[0]) == exhibition_id:
                exhibition = {
                    'exhibition_id': int(row[0]),
                    'title': row[1],
                    'description': row[2],
                    'gallery_id': row[3],
                    'exhibition_type': row[4],
                    'start_date': row[5],
                    'end_date': row[6],
                    'curator_name': row[7],
                }
                break
        if exhibition is None:
            abort(404)
        # Find artifacts for this exhibition
        artifacts_rows = read_pipe_delimited(ARTIFACTS_F)
        artifacts = []
        for art in artifacts_rows:
            if len(art) < 5:
                continue
            if art[3] == str(exhibition_id):
                artifacts.append({
                    'artifact_name': art[0],
                    'origin': art[1],
                    'description': art[2],
                    'storage_location': art[4],
                })
        return render_template('exhibition_details.html', exhibition=exhibition, artifacts=artifacts)

@app.route('/tickets', methods=['GET'])
def tickets():
    tickets_rows = read_pipe_delimited(TICKETS_F)
    tickets = []
    ticket_types = set()
    for t in tickets_rows:
        if len(t) < 6:
            continue
        tickets.append({
            'ticket_type': t[0],
            'visit_date': t[1],
            'visit_time': t[2],
            'visitor_name': t[3],
            'visitor_email': t[4],
            'purchase_date': t[5],
        })
        ticket_types.add(t[0])
    return render_template('visitor_tickets.html', tickets=tickets, ticket_types=sorted(ticket_types))

@app.route('/events', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def virtual_events():
    current_user = 'visitor_mary'
    events_rows = read_pipe_delimited(EVENTS_F)
    registrations_rows = read_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F)

    if request.method == 'POST':
        action = request.form.get('action')
        if action == 'cancel':
            registration_id = request.form.get('registration_id')
            if registration_id:
                registrations_rows = [r for r in registrations_rows if not (r[0] == registration_id and r[2] == current_user)]
                write_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F, registrations_rows)
            return redirect(url_for('virtual_events'))
        else:
            abort(400)

    virtual_events_list = []
    for e in events_rows:
        if len(e) < 7:
            continue
        virtual_events_list.append({
            'event_id': int(e[0]),
            'title': e[1],
            'date': e[2],
            'time': e[3],
            'event_type': e[4],
            'speaker': e[5],
            'capacity': e[6],
            'description': e[7] if len(e) > 7 else '',
        })

    regs_map = {int(r[1]): r[0] for r in registrations_rows if len(r) > 2 and r[2] == current_user}

    return render_template('virtual_events.html', events=virtual_events_list, registrations=regs_map, current_user=current_user)

@app.route('/events/register/<int:event_id>')
def register_event(event_id):
    current_user = 'visitor_mary'
    registrations_rows = read_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F)
    # Prevent duplicates
    for r in registrations_rows:
        if len(r) > 2 and r[1] == str(event_id) and r[2] == current_user:
            return redirect(url_for('virtual_events'))
    reg_ids = [int(r[0]) for r in registrations_rows if r[0].isdigit()]
    new_id = str(max(reg_ids) + 1 if reg_ids else 1)
    registration_date = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
    registrations_rows.append([new_id, str(event_id), current_user, registration_date])
    write_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F, registrations_rows)
    return redirect(url_for('virtual_events'))

@app.route('/events/cancel/<int:registration_id>', methods=['POST'])
def cancel_registration(registration_id):
    current_user = 'visitor_mary'
    registrations_rows = read_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F)
    registrations_rows = [r for r in registrations_rows if not (r[0] == str(registration_id) and r[2] == current_user)]
    write_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F, registrations_rows)
    return redirect(url_for('virtual_events'))

@app.route('/audio_guides', methods=['GET'])
def audio_guides():
    filter_language = request.args.get('filter_language','').lower()
    guides_rows = read_pipe_delimited(AUDIO_GUIDES_F)
    guides = []
    for g in guides_rows:
        if len(g) < 6:
            continue
        lang = g[3].lower()  # language field index corrected based on spec
        if filter_language and lang != filter_language:
            continue
        guides.append({
            'guide_id': g[0],
            'title': g[1],
            'narrator': g[4],
            'created_by': g[5]
        })
    return render_template('audio_guides.html', audio_guides=guides, filter_language=filter_language)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

=== app.py ===
from flask import Flask, redirect, url_for, request, render_template, abort
import os
from datetime import datetime

app = Flask(__name__)
app.secret_key = 'dev-secret-key'

DATA_DIR = "data"

# Paths
ARTIFACTS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "artifacts.txt")
EXHIBITIONS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "exhibitions.txt")
TICKETS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "tickets.txt")
EVENTS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "events.txt")
REGISTRATIONS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "event_registrations.txt")
AUDIO_GUIDES_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "audioguides.txt")

# Helpers

def read_pipe_delimited(filepath):
    if not os.path.exists(filepath):
        return []
    with open(filepath, encoding="utf-8") as f:
        return [line.strip().split('|') for line in f if line.strip()]

def write_pipe_delimited(filepath, rows):
    with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        for row in rows:
            f.write('|'.join(row)+'\n')

# Routes

@app.route('/')
def root_redirect():
    return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))

@app.route('/dashboard')
def dashboard():
    exhibitions = read_pipe_delimited(EXHIBITIONS_F)
    total_exhibitions = len(exhibitions)
    now = datetime.now().date()
    active_exhibitions = 0
    for ex in exhibitions:
        if len(ex) > 6:
            try:
                end_date = datetime.strptime(ex[6], '%Y-%m-%d').date()
                if end_date >= now:
                    active_exhibitions += 1
            except:
                pass
    return render_template('dashboard.html', total_exhibitions=total_exhibitions, active_exhibitions=active_exhibitions)

@app.route('/artifact_catalog', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def artifact_catalog():
    search_query = ''
    filters = {}
    if request.method == 'POST':
        search_query = request.form.get('search_query', '').strip()
    else:
        search_query = request.args.get('search_query', '').strip()
    # Filters from args
    for k,v in request.args.items():
        if k != 'search_query':
            filters[k] = v
    artifacts = []
    rows = read_pipe_delimited(ARTIFACTS_F)
    # artifact_name | origin | description | exhibition_id | storage_location
    for r in rows:
        if len(r) < 5:
            continue
        if search_query and search_query.lower() not in r[0].lower() and search_query.lower() not in r[3].lower():
            continue
        artifacts.append({
            'artifact_name': r[0],
            'origin': r[1],
            'description': r[2],
            'exhibition_id': r[3],
            'storage_location': r[4],
        })
    return render_template('artifact_catalog.html', artifacts=artifacts, search_query=search_query, filters=filters)

@app.route('/exhibitions', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def exhibitions():
    exhibitions_rows = read_pipe_delimited(EXHIBITIONS_F)
    exhibitions = []
    if request.method == 'GET':
        type_filter = request.args.get('filter_type','').lower()
        for row in exhibitions_rows:
            if len(row) < 8:
                continue
            if type_filter and row[4].lower() != type_filter:
                continue
            exhibitions.append({
                'exhibition_id': int(row[0]),
                'title': row[1],
                'description': row[2],
                'gallery_id': row[3],
                'exhibition_type': row[4],
                'start_date': row[5],
                'end_date': row[6],
                'curator_name': row[7],
            })
        return render_template('exhibitions.html', exhibitions=exhibitions, filter_type=type_filter)
    else:
        exhibition_id = request.form.get('exhibition_id')
        if not exhibition_id or not exhibition_id.isdigit():
            abort(400)
        exhibition_id = int(exhibition_id)
        exhibition = None
        for row in exhibitions_rows:
            if len(row)>0 and row[0].isdigit() and int(row[0]) == exhibition_id:
                exhibition = {
                    'exhibition_id': int(row[0]),
                    'title': row[1],
                    'description': row[2],
                    'gallery_id': row[3],
                    'exhibition_type': row[4],
                    'start_date': row[5],
                    'end_date': row[6],
                    'curator_name': row[7],
                }
                break
        if exhibition is None:
            abort(404)
        # Find artifacts for this exhibition
        artifacts_rows = read_pipe_delimited(ARTIFACTS_F)
        artifacts = []
        for art in artifacts_rows:
            if len(art) < 5:
                continue
            if art[3] == str(exhibition_id):
                artifacts.append({
                    'artifact_name': art[0],
                    'origin': art[1],
                    'description': art[2],
                    'storage_location': art[4],
                })
        return render_template('exhibition_details.html', exhibition=exhibition, artifacts=artifacts)

@app.route('/tickets', methods=['GET'])
def tickets():
    tickets_rows = read_pipe_delimited(TICKETS_F)
    tickets = []
    ticket_types = set()
    for t in tickets_rows:
        if len(t) < 6:
            continue
        tickets.append({
            'ticket_type': t[0],
            'visit_date': t[1],
            'visit_time': t[2],
            'visitor_name': t[3],
            'visitor_email': t[4],
            'purchase_date': t[5],
        })
        ticket_types.add(t[0])
    return render_template('visitor_tickets.html', tickets=tickets, ticket_types=sorted(ticket_types))

@app.route('/events', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
def virtual_events():
    current_user = 'visitor_mary'
    events_rows = read_pipe_delimited(EVENTS_F)
    registrations_rows = read_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F)

    if request.method == 'POST':
        action = request.form.get('action')
        if action == 'cancel':
            registration_id = request.form.get('registration_id')
            if registration_id:
                registrations_rows = [r for r in registrations_rows if not (r[0] == registration_id and r[2] == current_user)]
                write_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F, registrations_rows)
            return redirect(url_for('virtual_events'))
        else:
            abort(400)

    virtual_events_list = []
    for e in events_rows:
        if len(e) < 7:
            continue
        virtual_events_list.append({
            'event_id': int(e[0]),
            'title': e[1],
            'date': e[2],
            'time': e[3],
            'event_type': e[4],
            'speaker': e[5],
            'capacity': e[6],
            'description': e[7] if len(e) > 7 else '',
        })

    regs_map = {int(r[1]): r[0] for r in registrations_rows if len(r) > 2 and r[2] == current_user}

    return render_template('virtual_events.html', events=virtual_events_list, registrations=regs_map, current_user=current_user)

@app.route('/events/register/<int:event_id>')
def register_event(event_id):
    current_user = 'visitor_mary'
    registrations_rows = read_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F)
    # Prevent duplicates
    for r in registrations_rows:
        if len(r) > 2 and r[1] == str(event_id) and r[2] == current_user:
            return redirect(url_for('virtual_events'))
    reg_ids = [int(r[0]) for r in registrations_rows if r[0].isdigit()]
    new_id = str(max(reg_ids) + 1 if reg_ids else 1)
    registration_date = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
    registrations_rows.append([new_id, str(event_id), current_user, registration_date])
    write_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F, registrations_rows)
    return redirect(url_for('virtual_events'))

@app.route('/events/cancel/<int:registration_id>', methods=['POST'])
def cancel_registration(registration_id):
    current_user = 'visitor_mary'
    registrations_rows = read_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F)
    registrations_rows = [r for r in registrations_rows if not (r[0] == str(registration_id) and r[2] == current_user)]
    write_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F, registrations_rows)
    return redirect(url_for('virtual_events'))

@app.route('/audio_guides', methods=['GET'])
def audio_guides():
    filter_language = request.args.get('filter_language','').lower()
    guides_rows = read_pipe_delimited(AUDIO_GUIDES_F)
    guides = []
    for g in guides_rows:
        if len(g) < 6:
            continue
        lang = g[3].lower()  # language field index corrected based on spec
        if filter_language and lang != filter_language:
            continue
        guides.append({
            'guide_id': g[0],
            'title': g[1],
            'narrator': g[4],
            'created_by': g[5]
        })
    return render_template('audio_guides.html', audio_guides=guides, filter_language=filter_language)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

# Design Specification for VirtualMuseum Web Application

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

| Route Path                         | Function Name              | HTTP Method(s) | Template Rendered         | Context Variables (Name: Type)                                  |
|----------------------------------|----------------------------|----------------|---------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------|
| `/`                              | `root_redirect`             | GET            | Redirect to `/dashboard`  | None                                                           |
| `/dashboard`                     | `dashboard`                 | GET            | `dashboard.html`          | `total_exhibitions`: int, `active_exhibitions`: int           |
| `/artifacts`                     | `artifact_catalog`          | GET, POST      | `artifact_catalog.html`   | `artifacts`: list of dict, `search_query`: str, `filters`: dict|
| `/exhibitions`                   | `exhibitions`               | GET, POST      | `exhibitions.html`        | `exhibitions`: list of dict, `filter_type`: str                |
| `/exhibition/<int:exhibition_id>` | `exhibition_details`          | GET            | `exhibition_details.html` | `exhibition`: dict, `artifacts`: list of dict                  |
| `/tickets`                      | `visitor_tickets`           | GET, POST      | `visitor_tickets.html`    | `tickets`: list of dict, `ticket_types`: list of str           |
| `/events`                       | `virtual_events`            | GET, POST      | `virtual_events.html`     | `events`: list of dict, `registrations`: list of dict, `user`: str|
| `/events/register/<int:event_id>` | `register_event`             | POST           | Redirect to `/events`     | None                                                           |
| `/events/cancel/<int:registration_id>` | `cancel_registration`        | POST           | Redirect to `/events`     | None                                                           |
| `/audio-guides`                 | `audio_guides`              | GET, POST      | `audio_guides.html`       | `audio_guides`: list of dict, `filter_language`: str            |

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. `users.txt`
- Filename: `data/users.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `username`
- Purpose: Stores usernames authorized in the system.
- Examples:
  ```
  curator_john
  visitor_mary
  curator_sarah
  ```

---

### 2. `galleries.txt`
- Filename: `data/galleries.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `gallery_id`
  - `gallery_name`
  - `floor`
  - `capacity`
  - `theme`
  - `status`
- Purpose: Information about museum galleries.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|Ancient Civilizations Hall|1|50|Ancient|Open
  2|Modern Art Wing|2|30|Modern|Open
  3|Science Discovery Center|3|40|Science|Renovation
  ```

---

### 3. `exhibitions.txt`
- Filename: `data/exhibitions.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `exhibition_id`
  - `title`
  - `description`
  - `gallery_id`
  - `exhibition_type`
  - `start_date`
  - `end_date`
  - `curator_name`
  - `created_by`
- Purpose: Museum exhibitions data.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|Egyptian Treasures|Ancient artifacts from Egypt|1|Permanent|2024-01-01|2025-12-31|Dr. Smith|curator_john
  2|Pop Art Revolution|Contemporary pop art collection|2|Temporary|2024-11-01|2024-12-31|Lisa Chen|curator_sarah
  3|Virtual Space Exploration|Online space exhibition|2|Virtual|2024-10-01|2025-03-31|Mark Johnson|curator_john
  ```

---

### 4. `artifacts.txt`
- Filename: `data/artifacts.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `artifact_id`
  - `artifact_name`
  - `period`
  - `origin`
  - `description`
  - `exhibition_id`
  - `storage_location`
  - `acquisition_date`
  - `added_by`
- Purpose: Detailed artifact information.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|Golden Mask of Tutankhamun|Ancient|Egypt|Famous golden funeral mask|1|A-101|2020-05-15|curator_john
  2|Warhol Soup Cans|Contemporary|USA|Iconic pop art piece|2|B-205|2023-08-20|curator_sarah
  3|Roman Amphora|Ancient|Italy|Ancient storage vessel|1|A-103|2019-11-10|curator_john
  ```

---

### 5. `audioguides.txt`
- Filename: `data/audioguides.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `guide_id`
  - `exhibit_number`
  - `title`
  - `language`
  - `duration`
  - `script`
  - `narrator`
  - `created_by`
- Purpose: Audio guide content for exhibits.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|101|Introduction to Egyptian Art|English|5|Welcome to the Egyptian exhibition...|James Brown|curator_john
  2|101|Introducci  n al Arte Egipcio|Spanish|5|Bienvenido a la exhibici  n egipcia...|Maria Garcia|curator_john
  3|205|Pop Art Explained|English|7|Pop art emerged in the 1950s...|Sarah Williams|curator_sarah
  ```

---

### 6. `tickets.txt`
- Filename: `data/tickets.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `ticket_id`
  - `username`
  - `ticket_type`
  - `visit_date`
  - `visit_time`
  - `number_of_tickets`
  - `price`
  - `visitor_name`
  - `visitor_email`
  - `purchase_date`
- Purpose: Visitor ticket sales data.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|visitor_mary|Standard|2024-11-25|11:00 AM|2|30|Mary Johnson|mary@email.com|2024-11-20
  2|visitor_mary|VIP|2024-12-01|1:00 PM|1|50|Mary Johnson|mary@email.com|2024-11-20
  3|visitor_tom|Student|2024-11-22|9:00 AM|1|10|Tom Lee|tom@email.com|2024-11-18
  ```

---

### 7. `events.txt`
- Filename: `data/events.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `event_id`
  - `title`
  - `date`
  - `time`
  - `event_type`
  - `speaker`
  - `capacity`
  - `description`
  - `created_by`
- Purpose: Virtual museum events.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|Ancient Egypt Webinar|2024-12-05|2:00 PM|Webinar|Dr. Smith|100|Deep dive into Egyptian culture|curator_john
  2|Meet the Artist: Pop Art|2024-11-30|6:00 PM|Artist Talk|Andy Williams|50|Discussion with contemporary artist|curator_sarah
  3|Virtual Museum Tour|2024-12-10|10:00 AM|Virtual Tour|Lisa Chen|200|Guided tour of entire museum|curator_john
  ```

---

### 8. `event_registrations.txt`
- Filename: `data/event_registrations.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `registration_id`
  - `event_id`
  - `username`
  - `registration_date`
- Purpose: Records registrations for virtual events.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|1|visitor_mary|2024-11-20
  2|2|visitor_mary|2024-11-21
  3|1|visitor_tom|2024-11-19
  ```

---

### 9. `collection_logs.txt`
- Filename: `data/collection_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `log_id`
  - `artifact_id`
  - `activity_type`
  - `date`
  - `notes`
  - `condition`
  - `curator`
- Purpose: Logs artifact-related activities and condition.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|1|Inspection|2024-11-15|Routine quarterly inspection|Excellent|curator_john
  2|1|Cleaning|2024-11-16|Professional cleaning performed|Excellent|curator_john
  3|2|Photography|2024-10-20|High-resolution images taken|Good|curator_sarah
  4|3|Restoration|2024-09-10|Minor crack repair completed|Good|curator_john
  ```

---

*No ambiguities or missing information noted.*

2. [12:08:59] LLM_RESPONSE
   Response: ```python
from flask import Flask, redirect, url_for, request, render_template_string, abort
import os

app = Flask(__name__)
app.secret_key = 'dev-secret-key'

DATA_DIR = "data"

# File paths
GALLERIES_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "galleries.txt")
EXHIBITIONS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "exhibitions.txt")
ARTIFACTS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "artifacts.txt")
GUIDES_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "audio_guides.txt")
TICKETS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "tickets.txt")
EVENTS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "events.txt")
REGISTRATIONS_F = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, "event_registrations.txt")

# --- HELPER FUNCTIONS FOR FILE READING / WRITING ---

def read_pipe_delimited(filepath):
    """Read pipe-delimited file, return list of lists, skip empty lines."""
    if not os.path.exists(filepath):
        return []
    with open(filepath, encoding="utf-8") as f:
        lines = [line.strip() for line in f if line.strip()]
    rows = [line.split("|") for line in lines]
    return rows

def write_pipe_delimited(filepath, rows):
    """Write list of lists to pipe-delimited file."""
    with open(filepath, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for row in rows:
            f.write("|".join(row) + "\n")

# --- ROUTES ---

@app.route("/", methods=["GET"])
def root_redirect():
    # '/' GET Redirect to dashboard
    return redirect(url_for("dashboard"))

@app.route("/dashboard.html", methods=["GET"])
def dashboard():
    # Render dashboard.html page inline (no file reading)
    # Contains buttons with links per spec:
    # artifacts, exhibitions, visitor tickets, virtual events, audio guides
    
    # Inline minimal HTML with buttons linking to routes using url_for
    html = """
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    <head><title>Dashboard</title></head>
    <body>
      <h1>Dashboard</h1>
      <button id="artifact-catalog-button" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('artifact_catalog') }}'">Artifact Catalog</button>
      <button id="exhibitions-button" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('exhibitions') }}'">Exhibitions</button>
      <button id="visitor-tickets-button" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('visitor_tickets') }}'">Visitor Tickets</button>
      <button id="virtual-events-button" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('virtual_events') }}'">Virtual Events</button>
      <button id="audio-guides-button" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('audio_guides') }}'">Audio Guides</button>
    </body>
    </html>
    """
    return render_template_string(html)

@app.route("/artifacts", methods=["GET"])
def artifact_catalog():
    # List artifacts with optional filters
    # Parameters: search artifact name or ID, filters dict as query params (not detailed)
    # Load artifacts from artifacts.txt:
    # Fields: artifact_name | gallery_id | storage_location | date_acquired | created_by
    # Return minimal html with main H1: Artifact Catalog, artifact-table, search-artifact, apply-artifact-filter,
    # back-to-dashboard button
    
    artifacts_rows = read_pipe_delimited(ARTIFACTS_F)
    # filters could come from query params - we will accept one 'search' parameter for artifact_name or ID
    
    search = request.args.get("search", "").lower()
    
    # Filter artifacts by search if provided
    if search:
        filtered_artifacts = [row for row in artifacts_rows if search in row[0].lower() or search in row[1].lower()]
    else:
        filtered_artifacts = artifacts_rows
    
    # Render inline minimal HTML with table listing artifacts and form for searching, back to dashboard link
    
    html = """
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    <head><title>Artifact Catalog</title></head>
    <body>
      <h1>Artifact Catalog</h1>
      <form method="get" action="{{ url_for('artifact_catalog') }}">
        <input id="search-artifact" type="text" name="search" placeholder="Search artifact by name or gallery ID" value="{{ request.args.get('search','') }}">
        <button id="apply-artifact-filter" type="submit">Apply Filter</button>
      </form>
      <table id="artifact-table" border="1">
        <thead>
          <tr><th>Artifact Name</th><th>Gallery ID</th><th>Storage Location</th><th>Date Acquired</th><th>Created By</th></tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>
        {% for art in artifacts %}
          <tr>
            <td>{{ art[0] }}</td>
            <td>{{ art[1] }}</td>
            <td>{{ art[2] }}</td>
            <td>{{ art[3] }}</td>
            <td>{{ art[4] }}</td>
          </tr>
        {% endfor %}
        </tbody>
      </table>
      <button id="back-to-dashboard" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('dashboard') }}'">Back to Dashboard</button>
    </body>
    </html>
    """
    return render_template_string(html, artifacts=filtered_artifacts, request=request)

@app.route("/exhibitions", methods=["GET", "POST"])
def exhibitions():
    # GET: show list of exhibitions with filter options
    # POST: show exhibition_details.html for a specific exhibition with artifacts etc.
    if request.method == "GET":
        # read exhibitions and display with filter-exhibition-type filter and apply-exhibition-filter button and back-to-dashboard
        
        exhibitions_rows = read_pipe_delimited(EXHIBITIONS_F)
        # Fields of exhibitions.txt:
        # exhibition_id | title | gallery_id | exhibition_type | start_date | end_date | created_by
        
        # Optional filter by exhibition_type from query param 'filter_type'
        filter_type = request.args.get("filter_type", "").lower()
        if filter_type:
            filtered_exhibitions = [row for row in exhibitions_rows if len(row)>3 and filter_type == row[3].lower()]
        else:
            filtered_exhibitions = exhibitions_rows
        
        html = """
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
        <head><title>Exhibitions</title></head>
        <body>
          <h1>Exhibitions</h1>
          <form method="get" action="{{ url_for('exhibitions') }}">
            <select id="filter-exhibition-type" name="filter_type">
              <option value="" {% if not filter_type %}selected{% endif %}>All Types</option>
              <option value="Temporary" {% if filter_type=='temporary' %}selected{% endif %}>Temporary</option>
              <option value="Permanent" {% if filter_type=='permanent' %}selected{% endif %}>Permanent</option>
              <option value="Virtual" {% if filter_type=='virtual' %}selected{% endif %}>Virtual</option>
              <!-- Add other types as needed -->
            </select>
            <button id="apply-exhibition-filter" type="submit">Apply Filter</button>
          </form>
          <ul>
          {% for ex in exhibitions %}
            <li>
              <form method="post" action="{{ url_for('exhibitions') }}" style="display:inline;">
                <input type="hidden" name="exhibition_id" value="{{ ex[0] }}">
                <button type="submit">{{ ex[1] }}</button> (Type: {{ ex[3] }})
              </form>
            </li>
          {% endfor %}
          </ul>
          <button id="back-to-dashboard" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('dashboard') }}'">Back to Dashboard</button>
        </body>
        </html>
        """
        return render_template_string(html, exhibitions=filtered_exhibitions, filter_type=filter_type)
    else:
        # POST: exhibition_details.html for given exhibition_id
        exhibition_id = request.form.get("exhibition_id", "")
        # Validate exhibition_id present in exhibitions file
        exhibitions_rows = read_pipe_delimited(EXHIBITIONS_F)
        exhibition = None
        for ex in exhibitions_rows:
            if ex and ex[0] == exhibition_id:
                exhibition = ex
                break
        if not exhibition:
            abort(404, description="Exhibition not found")
        
        # Get exhibition details: show title, description, dates, and list artifacts for this exhibition
        # exhibition fields as per spec: exhibition_id | title | gallery_id | type | start_date | end_date | created_by
        # For artifacts, match artifacts with gallery_id = exhibition's gallery_id
        
        artifacts_rows = read_pipe_delimited(ARTIFACTS_F)
        exhibition_artifacts = [a for a in artifacts_rows if len(a)>1 and a[1] == exhibition[2]]
        
        html = """
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
        <head><title>Exhibition Details</title></head>
        <body>
          <h1>{{ exhibition[1] }}</h1>
          <p><b>Description:</b> {{ exhibition[1] }}</p>
          <p><b>Gallery ID:</b> {{ exhibition[2] }}</p>
          <p><b>Type:</b> {{ exhibition[3] }}</p>
          <p><b>Start Date:</b> {{ exhibition[4] }}</p>
          <p><b>End Date:</b> {{ exhibition[5] }}</p>
          <p><b>Created By:</b> {{ exhibition[6] }}</p>
          
          <h2>Artifacts</h2>
          <table border="1">
            <thead>
              <tr><th>Artifact Name</th><th>Storage Location</th><th>Date Acquired</th><th>Created By</th></tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
            {% for art in artifacts %}
              <tr>
                <td>{{ art[0] }}</td>
                <td>{{ art[2] }}</td>
                <td>{{ art[3] }}</td>
                <td>{{ art[4] }}</td>
              </tr>
            {% endfor %}
            </tbody>
          </table>
          
          <button id="back-to-exhibitions" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('exhibitions') }}'">Back to Exhibitions</button>
        </body>
        </html>
        """
        return render_template_string(html, exhibition=exhibition, artifacts=exhibition_artifacts)

@app.route("/virtual_events", methods=["GET", "POST"])
def virtual_events():
    # GET: list virtual events
    # POST: registration-related actions (register or cancel)
    # Context: user events registrations data
    
    # For demo, assume a user 'visitor_mary'
    current_user = "visitor_mary"
    
    events_rows = read_pipe_delimited(EVENTS_F)
    # Fields: event_id | title | date | event_type | description | created_by
    
    registrations_rows = read_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F)
    # Fields: registration_id | event_id | user | registration_date
    
    user_regs = {reg[1]: reg[0] for reg in registrations_rows if len(reg) > 2 and reg[2] == current_user}
    # key = event_id, value = registration_id
    
    if request.method == "POST":
        # distinguish action by form field or value
        action = request.form.get("action", "")
        if action == "register":
            event_id = request.form.get("event_id", "")
            # Prevent duplicate
            if event_id in user_regs:
                pass  # already registered
            else:
                # Create new registration_id (max+1 or 1)
                reg_ids = [int(r[0]) for r in registrations_rows if r and r[0].isdigit()]
                new_reg_id = str(max(reg_ids)+1 if reg_ids else 1)
                from datetime import datetime
                registration_date = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
                new_reg = [new_reg_id, event_id, current_user, registration_date]
                registrations_rows.append(new_reg)
                write_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F, registrations_rows)
            return redirect(url_for('virtual_events'))
        elif action == "cancel":
            registration_id = request.form.get("registration_id", "")
            # Remove that registration if owned by current_user
            registrations_rows = [r for r in registrations_rows if not (r[0] == registration_id and r[2] == current_user)]
            write_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F, registrations_rows)
            return redirect(url_for('virtual_events'))
        else:
            abort(400, description="Invalid action")
    else:
        # GET list all virtual events (event_type 'Virtual' only)
        virtual_events_list = [e for e in events_rows if len(e)>3 and e[3].lower() == 'virtual']
        # Build registrations dict: event_id -> registration_id or None
        regs_dict = {}
        for ev in virtual_events_list:
            eid = ev[0]
            regs_dict[eid] = user_regs.get(eid)
        
        html = """
        <!DOCTYPE html>
        <html>
        <head><title>Virtual Events</title></head>
        <body>
          <h1>Virtual Events</h1>
          <ul id="event-list">
          {% for ev in events %}
            <li>
              <b>{{ ev[1] }}</b> - {{ ev[2] }}<br>
              {{ ev[4] }}<br>
              {% if registrations[ev[0]] %}
              <form method="post" style="display:inline;">
                <input type="hidden" name="action" value="cancel">
                <input type="hidden" name="registration_id" value="{{ registrations[ev[0]] }}">
                <button id="cancel-registration-button-{{ registrations[ev[0]] }}" type="submit">Cancel Registration</button>
              </form>
              {% else %}
              <form method="post" style="display:inline;">
                <input type="hidden" name="action" value="register">
                <input type="hidden" name="event_id" value="{{ ev[0] }}">
                <button id="register-event-button-{{ ev[0] }}" type="submit">Register</button>
              </form>
              {% endif %}
            </li>
          {% endfor %}
          </ul>
          <button onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('dashboard') }}'">Back to Dashboard</button>
        </body>
        </html>
        """
        return render_template_string(html, events=virtual_events_list, registrations=regs_dict)

@app.route("/audio_guides", methods=["GET"])
def audio_guides():
    # GET list audio guides with optional filter_language query param
    
    filter_language = request.args.get("filter_language", "").lower()
    
    guides_rows = read_pipe_delimited(GUIDES_F)
    # Fields: guide_id | exhibit_number | text_content | narrator | created_by
    
    # For language field, guessing based on example in spec, 
    # Spec shows language field, but sample rows have unclear order.
    # Given spec fields at 5:
    # guide_id | exhibit_number | language | text_content | narrator | created_by
    # Examples given seem to have language as 3rd element maybe
    # We'll assume field order: guide_id | exhibit_number | language | text_content | narrator | created_by
    
    filtered_guides = []
    for g in guides_rows:
        if len(g) < 6:
            continue
        lang = g[2].lower()
        if filter_language and lang != filter_language:
            continue
        filtered_guides.append(g)
    
    html = """
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    <head><title>Audio Guides</title></head>
    <body>
      <h1>Audio Guides</h1>
      <form method="get" action="{{ url_for('audio_guides') }}">
        <label for="filter-language">Filter language:</label>
        <input id="filter-language" type="text" name="filter_language" value="{{ request.args.get('filter_language','') }}">
        <button type="submit">Apply Filter</button>
      </form>
      <ul id="audio-guide-list">
      {% for g in guides %}
        <li>
          Guide ID: {{ g[0] }}, Exhibit #: {{ g[1] }}, Language: {{ g[2] }}, Narrator: {{ g[4] }}
          <button id="play-guide-button-{{ g[0] }}">Play Guide</button>
          <p>{{ g[3] }}</p>
        </li>
      {% endfor %}
      </ul>
      <button onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('dashboard') }}'">Back to Dashboard</button>
    </body>
    </html>
    """
    return render_template_string(html, guides=filtered_guides, request=request)

@app.route("/visitor_tickets", methods=["GET"])
def visitor_tickets():
    # GET visitor tickets: show purchased tickets and ticket types
    # Spec says 'Visitor Tickets' page with ticket-type element, my-tickets-table, back button
    # Tickets file fields: visit_date | visit_time | number_of_tickets | visitor_email | purchase_date
    
    # For minimal demo, assume current user email or username 'visitor_mary'
    visitor_username = "visitor_mary"
    
    tickets_rows = read_pipe_delimited(TICKETS_F)
    # Tickets are stored by visitor_email or visitor username. Spec examples mix:
    # Possibly visitor_email is key, but we do not have mapping username -> email.
    # Will show all tickets without filtering (no user identification)
    
    # Just list all tickets with fields per spec
    # Let's show from tickets.txt all tickets with visitor_email == visitor_username or visitor_email containing visitor_username
    
    # But specimen lines show visitor_email field possibly as second or fourth field? Spec unclear somewhat.
    # Spec fields (pipe delimited) in tickets.txt:
    # visit_date | visit_time | number_of_tickets | visitor_email | purchase_date
    
    filtered_tickets = [t for t in tickets_rows if len(t) > 3 and visitor_username in t[3]]
    
    ticket_types = set()
    for t in filtered_tickets:
        # No ticket type on ticket line in spec - so we cannot show types from tickets
        # Spec for ticket types is vague; skip or show limited info
        pass
    
    html = """
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    <head><title>Visitor Tickets</title></head>
    <body>
      <h1>Visitor Tickets</h1>
      <p>Ticket types info not available in spec</p>
      <table id="my-tickets-table" border="1">
        <thead>
          <tr><th>Visit Date</th><th>Visit Time</th><th>Number of Tickets</th><th>Visitor Email</th><th>Purchase Date</th></tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>
        {% for ticket in tickets %}
          <tr>
            <td>{{ ticket[0] }}</td>
            <td>{{ ticket[1] }}</td>
            <td>{{ ticket[2] }}</td>
            <td>{{ ticket[3] }}</td>
            <td>{{ ticket[4] }}</td>
          </tr>
        {% endfor %}
        </tbody>
      </table>
      <button id="back-to-dashboard" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('dashboard') }}'">Back to Dashboard</button>
    </body>
    </html>
    """
    return render_template_string(html, tickets=filtered_tickets)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app.run(port=5000, debug=True)

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. `users.txt`
- Filename: `data/users.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `username`
- Purpose: Stores usernames authorized in the system.
- Examples:
  ```
  curator_john
  visitor_mary
  curator_sarah
  ```

---

### 2. `galleries.txt`
- Filename: `data/galleries.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `gallery_id`
  - `gallery_name`
  - `floor`
  - `capacity`
  - `theme`
  - `status`
- Purpose: Information about museum galleries.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|Ancient Civilizations Hall|1|50|Ancient|Open
  2|Modern Art Wing|2|30|Modern|Open
  3|Science Discovery Center|3|40|Science|Renovation
  ```

---

### 3. `exhibitions.txt`
- Filename: `data/exhibitions.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `exhibition_id`
  - `title`
  - `description`
  - `gallery_id`
  - `exhibition_type`
  - `start_date`
  - `end_date`
  - `curator_name`
  - `created_by`
- Purpose: Museum exhibitions data.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|Egyptian Treasures|Ancient artifacts from Egypt|1|Permanent|2024-01-01|2025-12-31|Dr. Smith|curator_john
  2|Pop Art Revolution|Contemporary pop art collection|2|Temporary|2024-11-01|2024-12-31|Lisa Chen|curator_sarah
  3|Virtual Space Exploration|Online space exhibition|2|Virtual|2024-10-01|2025-03-31|Mark Johnson|curator_john
  ```

---

### 4. `artifacts.txt`
- Filename: `data/artifacts.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `artifact_id`
  - `artifact_name`
  - `period`
  - `origin`
  - `description`
  - `exhibition_id`
  - `storage_location`
  - `acquisition_date`
  - `added_by`
- Purpose: Detailed artifact information.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|Golden Mask of Tutankhamun|Ancient|Egypt|Famous golden funeral mask|1|A-101|2020-05-15|curator_john
  2|Warhol Soup Cans|Contemporary|USA|Iconic pop art piece|2|B-205|2023-08-20|curator_sarah
  3|Roman Amphora|Ancient|Italy|Ancient storage vessel|1|A-103|2019-11-10|curator_john
  ```

---

### 5. `audioguides.txt`
- Filename: `data/audioguides.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `guide_id`
  - `exhibit_number`
  - `title`
  - `language`
  - `duration`
  - `script`
  - `narrator`
  - `created_by`
- Purpose: Audio guide content for exhibits.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|101|Introduction to Egyptian Art|English|5|Welcome to the Egyptian exhibition...|James Brown|curator_john
  2|101|Introducci  n al Arte Egipcio|Spanish|5|Bienvenido a la exhibici  n egipcia...|Maria Garcia|curator_john
  3|205|Pop Art Explained|English|7|Pop art emerged in the 1950s...|Sarah Williams|curator_sarah
  ```

---

### 6. `tickets.txt`
- Filename: `data/tickets.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `ticket_id`
  - `username`
  - `ticket_type`
  - `visit_date`
  - `visit_time`
  - `number_of_tickets`
  - `price`
  - `visitor_name`
  - `visitor_email`
  - `purchase_date`
- Purpose: Visitor ticket sales data.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|visitor_mary|Standard|2024-11-25|11:00 AM|2|30|Mary Johnson|mary@email.com|2024-11-20
  2|visitor_mary|VIP|2024-12-01|1:00 PM|1|50|Mary Johnson|mary@email.com|2024-11-20
  3|visitor_tom|Student|2024-11-22|9:00 AM|1|10|Tom Lee|tom@email.com|2024-11-18
  ```

---

### 7. `events.txt`
- Filename: `data/events.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `event_id`
  - `title`
  - `date`
  - `time`
  - `event_type`
  - `speaker`
  - `capacity`
  - `description`
  - `created_by`
- Purpose: Virtual museum events.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|Ancient Egypt Webinar|2024-12-05|2:00 PM|Webinar|Dr. Smith|100|Deep dive into Egyptian culture|curator_john
  2|Meet the Artist: Pop Art|2024-11-30|6:00 PM|Artist Talk|Andy Williams|50|Discussion with contemporary artist|curator_sarah
  3|Virtual Museum Tour|2024-12-10|10:00 AM|Virtual Tour|Lisa Chen|200|Guided tour of entire museum|curator_john
  ```

---

### 8. `event_registrations.txt`
- Filename: `data/event_registrations.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `registration_id`
  - `event_id`
  - `username`
  - `registration_date`
- Purpose: Records registrations for virtual events.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|1|visitor_mary|2024-11-20
  2|2|visitor_mary|2024-11-21
  3|1|visitor_tom|2024-11-19
  ```

---

### 9. `collection_logs.txt`
- Filename: `data/collection_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `log_id`
  - `artifact_id`
  - `activity_type`
  - `date`
  - `notes`
  - `condition`
  - `curator`
- Purpose: Logs artifact-related activities and condition.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|1|Inspection|2024-11-15|Routine quarterly inspection|Excellent|curator_john
  2|1|Cleaning|2024-11-16|Professional cleaning performed|Excellent|curator_john
  3|2|Photography|2024-10-20|High-resolution images taken|Good|curator_sarah
  4|3|Restoration|2024-09-10|Minor crack repair completed|Good|curator_john
  ```

---

*No ambiguities or missing information noted.*
