For filters, assume keys come as filter_key=value\n    for key in request.args:\n        if key != \"search_query\":\n            filters[key] = request.args.get(key)\n    artifacts = []\n    rows = read_pipe_delimited(ARTIFACTS_F)\n    # fields: artifact_name|gallery_id|storage_location|date_acquired|created_by\n    for r in rows:\n        if len(r) < 5:\n            continue\n        if search_query:\n            if search_query.lower() not in r[0].lower() and search_query.lower() not in r[1].lower():\n                continue\n        # TODO: apply other filters if any\n        artifacts.append({\n            \"artifact_name\": r[0],\n            \"gallery_id\": r[1],\n            \"storage_location\": r[2],\n            \"date_acquired\": r[3],\n            \"created_by\": r[4],\n        })\n    return render_template(\"artifact_catalog.html\", artifacts=artifacts, search_query=search_query, filters=filters)\n\n@app.route(\"/exhibition/<int:exhibition_id>\", methods=[\"GET\"])\ndef exhibition_details(exhibition_id):\n    exhibitions = read_pipe_delimited(EXHIBITIONS_F)\n    exhibition = None\n    for ex in exhibitions:\n        try:\n            if int(ex[0]) == exhibition_id:\n                exhibition = ex\n                break\n        except Exception:\n            continue\n    if exhibition is None:\n        abort(404, \"Exhibition not found\")\n\n    # fields: exhibition_id|title|description|gallery_id|exhibition_type|start_date|end_date|curator_name\n    artifacts_rows = read_pipe_delimited(ARTIFACTS_F)\n    artifacts = []\n    gallery_id = exhibition[3] if len(exhibition) > 3 else \"\"\n    for art in artifacts_rows:\n        if len(art) > 1 and art[1] == gallery_id:\n            artifacts.append({\n                \"artifact_name\": art[0],\n                \"storage_location\": art[2],\n                \"date_acquired\": art[3],\n                \"created_by\": art[4],\n            })\n\n    exhibition_dict = {\n        \"exhibition_id\": exhibition[0],\n        \"title\": exhibition[1],\n        \"description\": exhibition[2],\n        \"gallery_id\": exhibition[3],\n        \"exhibition_type\": exhibition[4],\n        \"start_date\": exhibition[5],\n        \"end_date\": exhibition[6],\n        \"curator_name\": exhibition[7] if len(exhibition) > 7 else \"\"\n    }\n    return render_template(\"exhibition_details.html\", exhibition=exhibition_dict, artifacts=artifacts)\n\n@app.route(\"/tickets\", methods=[\"GET\"])\ndef visitor_tickets():\n    # tickets.txt fields:\n    # visit_date|visit_time|number_of_tickets|visitor_name|visitor_email|purchase_date\n    tickets_rows = read_pipe_delimited(TICKETS_F)\n    ticket_types = set()\n    tickets = []\n    for t in tickets_rows:\n        if len(t) < 6:\n            continue\n        tickets.append({\n            \"visit_date\": t[0],\n            \"visit_time\": t[1],\n            \"number_of_tickets\": t[2],\n            \"visitor_name\": t[3],\n            \"visitor_email\": t[4],\n            \"purchase_date\": t[5]\n        })\n        ticket_types.add(t[2])\n\n    ticket_types = list(ticket_types)\n    return render_template(\"visitor_tickets.html\", tickets=tickets, ticket_types=ticket_types)\n\n@app.route(\"/events\", methods=[\"GET\", \"POST\"])\ndef virtual_events():\n    current_user = \"visitor_mary\"  # TODO: authentication placeholder\n    events_rows = read_pipe_delimited(EVENTS_F)\n    registrations_rows = read_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F)\n\n    if request.method == \"POST\":\n        # Either register or cancel\n        action = request.form.get(\"action\")\n        if action == \"cancel\":\n            registration_id = request.form.get(\"registration_id\")\n            if registration_id:\n                registrations_rows = [r for r in registrations_rows if r[0] != registration_id or r[2] != current_user]\n                write_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F, registrations_rows)\n            return redirect(url_for(\"virtual_events\"))\n        else:\n            abort(400)\n\n    # On GET, list virtual events\n    virtual_events_list = []\n    for e in events_rows:\n        if len(e) < 7:\n            continue\n        event_type = e[4].lower()\n        if event_type == \"virtual\":\n            virtual_events_list.append({\n                \"event_id\": e[0],\n                \"title\": e[1],\n                \"date\": e[2],\n                \"time\": e[3],\n                \"event_type\": e[4],\n                \"speaker\": e[5],\n                \"seats\": e[6] if len(e) > 6 else \"\",\n                \"description\": e[7] if len(e) > 7 else \"\"\n            })\n\n    # Map registrations for current user: event_id -> registration_id\n    regs_map = {r[1]: r[0] for r in registrations_rows if len(r) > 2 and r[2] == current_user}\n\n    return render_template(\"virtual_events.html\", events=virtual_events_list, registrations=regs_map, current_user=current_user)\n\n@app.route(\"/events/register/<int:event_id>\", methods=[\"GET\"])\ndef register_event(event_id):\n    current_user = \"visitor_mary\"\n    registrations_rows = read_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F)\n    # Check if already registered\n    for r in registrations_rows:\n        if len(r) > 2 and r[1] == str(event_id) and r[2] == current_user:\n            return redirect(url_for(\"virtual_events\"))\n    reg_ids = [int(r[0]) for r in registrations_rows if r[0].isdigit()]\n    new_id = str(max(reg_ids)+1 if reg_ids else 1)\n    registration_date = datetime.now().strftime(\"%Y-%m-%d\")\n    registrations_rows.append([new_id, str(event_id), current_user, registration_date])\n    write_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F, registrations_rows)\n    return redirect(url_for(\"virtual_events\"))\n\n@app.route(\"/events/cancel/<int:registration_id>\", methods=[\"POST\"])\ndef cancel_registration(registration_id):\n    current_user = \"visitor_mary\"\n    registrations_rows = read_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F)\n    new_regs = [r for r in registrations_rows if not (r[0] == str(registration_id) and r[2] == current_user)]\n    write_pipe_delimited(REGISTRATIONS_F, new_regs)\n    return redirect(url_for(\"virtual_events\"))\n\n@app.route(\"/audio_guides\", methods=[\"GET\"])\ndef audio_guides():\n    filter_language = request.args.get(\"filter_language\", \"\").lower()\n    guides_rows = read_pipe_delimited(GUIDES_F)\n    guides = []\n    for g in guides_rows:\n        # # Design Specification for VirtualMuseum Web Application

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

| Route Path                         | Function Name              | HTTP Method(s) | Template Rendered         | Context Variables (Name: Type)                                  |
|----------------------------------|----------------------------|----------------|---------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------|
| `/`                              | `root_redirect`             | GET            | Redirect to `/dashboard`  | None                                                           |
| `/dashboard`                     | `dashboard`                 | GET            | `dashboard.html`          | `total_exhibitions`: int, `active_exhibitions`: int           |
| `/artifacts`                     | `artifact_catalog`          | GET, POST      | `artifact_catalog.html`   | `artifacts`: list of dict, `search_query`: str, `filters`: dict|
| `/exhibitions`                   | `exhibitions`               | GET, POST      | `exhibitions.html`        | `exhibitions`: list of dict, `filter_type`: str                |
| `/exhibition/<int:exhibition_id>` | `exhibition_details`          | GET            | `exhibition_details.html` | `exhibition`: dict, `artifacts`: list of dict                  |
| `/tickets`                      | `visitor_tickets`           | GET, POST      | `visitor_tickets.html`    | `tickets`: list of dict, `ticket_types`: list of str           |
| `/events`                       | `virtual_events`            | GET, POST      | `virtual_events.html`     | `events`: list of dict, `registrations`: list of dict, `user`: str|
| `/events/register/<int:event_id>` | `register_event`             | POST           | Redirect to `/events`     | None                                                           |
| `/events/cancel/<int:registration_id>` | `cancel_registration`        | POST           | Redirect to `/events`     | None                                                           |
| `/audio-guides`                 | `audio_guides`              | GET, POST      | `audio_guides.html`       | `audio_guides`: list of dict, `filter_language`: str            |

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. `users.txt`
- Filename: `data/users.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `username`
- Purpose: Stores usernames authorized in the system.
- Examples:
  ```
  curator_john
  visitor_mary
  curator_sarah
  ```

---

### 2. `galleries.txt`
- Filename: `data/galleries.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `gallery_id`
  - `gallery_name`
  - `floor`
  - `capacity`
  - `theme`
  - `status`
- Purpose: Information about museum galleries.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|Ancient Civilizations Hall|1|50|Ancient|Open
  2|Modern Art Wing|2|30|Modern|Open
  3|Science Discovery Center|3|40|Science|Renovation
  ```

---

### 3. `exhibitions.txt`
- Filename: `data/exhibitions.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `exhibition_id`
  - `title`
  - `description`
  - `gallery_id`
  - `exhibition_type`
  - `start_date`
  - `end_date`
  - `curator_name`
  - `created_by`
- Purpose: Museum exhibitions data.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|Egyptian Treasures|Ancient artifacts from Egypt|1|Permanent|2024-01-01|2025-12-31|Dr. Smith|curator_john
  2|Pop Art Revolution|Contemporary pop art collection|2|Temporary|2024-11-01|2024-12-31|Lisa Chen|curator_sarah
  3|Virtual Space Exploration|Online space exhibition|2|Virtual|2024-10-01|2025-03-31|Mark Johnson|curator_john
  ```

---

### 4. `artifacts.txt`
- Filename: `data/artifacts.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `artifact_id`
  - `artifact_name`
  - `period`
  - `origin`
  - `description`
  - `exhibition_id`
  - `storage_location`
  - `acquisition_date`
  - `added_by`
- Purpose: Detailed artifact information.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|Golden Mask of Tutankhamun|Ancient|Egypt|Famous golden funeral mask|1|A-101|2020-05-15|curator_john
  2|Warhol Soup Cans|Contemporary|USA|Iconic pop art piece|2|B-205|2023-08-20|curator_sarah
  3|Roman Amphora|Ancient|Italy|Ancient storage vessel|1|A-103|2019-11-10|curator_john
  ```

---

### 5. `audioguides.txt`
- Filename: `data/audioguides.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `guide_id`
  - `exhibit_number`
  - `title`
  - `language`
  - `duration`
  - `script`
  - `narrator`
  - `created_by`
- Purpose: Audio guide content for exhibits.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|101|Introduction to Egyptian Art|English|5|Welcome to the Egyptian exhibition...|James Brown|curator_john
  2|101|Introducci  n al Arte Egipcio|Spanish|5|Bienvenido a la exhibici  n egipcia...|Maria Garcia|curator_john
  3|205|Pop Art Explained|English|7|Pop art emerged in the 1950s...|Sarah Williams|curator_sarah
  ```

---

### 6. `tickets.txt`
- Filename: `data/tickets.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `ticket_id`
  - `username`
  - `ticket_type`
  - `visit_date`
  - `visit_time`
  - `number_of_tickets`
  - `price`
  - `visitor_name`
  - `visitor_email`
  - `purchase_date`
- Purpose: Visitor ticket sales data.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|visitor_mary|Standard|2024-11-25|11:00 AM|2|30|Mary Johnson|mary@email.com|2024-11-20
  2|visitor_mary|VIP|2024-12-01|1:00 PM|1|50|Mary Johnson|mary@email.com|2024-11-20
  3|visitor_tom|Student|2024-11-22|9:00 AM|1|10|Tom Lee|tom@email.com|2024-11-18
  ```

---

### 7. `events.txt`
- Filename: `data/events.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `event_id`
  - `title`
  - `date`
  - `time`
  - `event_type`
  - `speaker`
  - `capacity`
  - `description`
  - `created_by`
- Purpose: Virtual museum events.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|Ancient Egypt Webinar|2024-12-05|2:00 PM|Webinar|Dr. Smith|100|Deep dive into Egyptian culture|curator_john
  2|Meet the Artist: Pop Art|2024-11-30|6:00 PM|Artist Talk|Andy Williams|50|Discussion with contemporary artist|curator_sarah
  3|Virtual Museum Tour|2024-12-10|10:00 AM|Virtual Tour|Lisa Chen|200|Guided tour of entire museum|curator_john
  ```

---

### 8. `event_registrations.txt`
- Filename: `data/event_registrations.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `registration_id`
  - `event_id`
  - `username`
  - `registration_date`
- Purpose: Records registrations for virtual events.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|1|visitor_mary|2024-11-20
  2|2|visitor_mary|2024-11-21
  3|1|visitor_tom|2024-11-19
  ```

---

### 9. `collection_logs.txt`
- Filename: `data/collection_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  - `log_id`
  - `artifact_id`
  - `activity_type`
  - `date`
  - `notes`
  - `condition`
  - `curator`
- Purpose: Logs artifact-related activities and condition.
- Examples:
  ```
  1|1|Inspection|2024-11-15|Routine quarterly inspection|Excellent|curator_john
  2|1|Cleaning|2024-11-16|Professional cleaning performed|Excellent|curator_john
  3|2|Photography|2024-10-20|High-resolution images taken|Good|curator_sarah
  4|3|Restoration|2024-09-10|Minor crack repair completed|Good|curator_john
  ```

---

*No ambiguities or missing information noted.*
